## user

Implement the following plan:

# Implementation Plan: Self-Learning Rails MCP Server

## Overview

Build a TypeScript MCP server for Rails + React + PostgreSQL development that:
1. Guides users through workflows with questions/options
2. Generates code from templates and snippets
3. Learns from successful implementations
4. Analyzes existing apps to bootstrap the library

**Project Location:** `/home/joseph/mcp-servers/rails-dev-mcp`
**Tech Stack:** TypeScript MCP server, React with TypeScript frontend analysis
**Initial Bootstrap:** 6+ existing apps to analyze for pattern extraction

---

## Phase 1: Project Setup & Core Infrastructure

### 1.1 Initialize MCP Server Project

**Directory:** `/home/joseph/mcp-servers/rails-dev-mcp`

```
rails-dev-mcp/
├── package.json
├── tsconfig.json
├── src/
│   ├── index.ts                    # MCP server entry point
│   ├── server.ts                   # Server configuration
│   ├── tools/                      # MCP tool definitions
│   ├── engines/                    # Core logic engines
│   ├── parsers/                    # Code parsers (Ruby, TS, CSS)
│   └── utils/                      # Shared utilities
├── library/                        # Knowledge base
│   ├── patterns/
│   ├── templates/
│   ├── snippets/
│   ├── queries/
│   └── learned/
├── config/
│   └── default.yml
└── tests/
```

**Dependencies:**
- `@modelcontextprotocol/sdk` - MCP server SDK
- `pg` - PostgreSQL client
- `@babel/parser` + `@babel/traverse` - React/TS parsing
- `tree-sitter` + `tree-sitter-ruby` - Ruby parsing
- `postcss` - CSS parsing
- `yaml` - Configuration
- `glob` - File discovery
- `ejs` - Template rendering
- `simple-git` - Git operations for remote repos

### 1.2 Core Data Structures

Create TypeScript interfaces for:
- `Pattern` - workflow definitions
- `Template` - code templates with variables
- `Snippet` - reusable code fragments
- `Workflow` - runtime workflow state
- `ProjectContext` - detected project configuration
- `Contribution` - learned pattern candidates

---

## Phase 2: Workflow Engine

### 2.1 Intent Identification Tool

**Tool:** `identify_intent`

- Load all pattern manifests from library
- Score user prompt against pattern triggers
- Return matched pattern or clarifying questions

### 2.2 Workflow Execution Tools

**Tool:** `start_workflow`
- Load workflow definition for pattern
- Detect project context (models, components, gems)
- Return first question with pre-selected recommendations

**Tool:** `answer_workflow_step`
- Store answer, evaluate conditions
- Return next question or ready-to-execute summary

**Tool:** `execute_workflow`
- Resolve templates based on answers
- Generate files using template engine
- Return created files and next steps

### 2.3 Workflow Definition Schema

```typescript
interface WorkflowStep {
  id: string;
  question: string;
  type: 'single_select' | 'multi_select' | 'text' | 'confirm';
  options?: WorkflowOption[];
  condition?: string;  // JavaScript expression
  affects: ('templates' | 'snippets' | 'instructions')[];
}
```

---

## Phase 3: Template Engine

### 3.1 Template Format

Use EJS templates with convention helpers:

```ejs
// templates/model.rb.ejs
class <%= modelName %> < ApplicationRecord
<% if (associations.belongsTo) { %>
<% associations.belongsTo.forEach(assoc => { %>
  belongs_to :<%= assoc %>
<% }) %>
<% } %>
<% if (validations.presence) { %>
  validates <%= validations.presence.map(f => `:${f}`).join(', ') %>, presence: true
<% } %>
end
```

### 3.2 Template Tools

**Tool:** `get_template` - Retrieve and render a template
**Tool:** `list_templates` - Browse available templates
**Tool:** `preview_template` - Render with sample data

---

## Phase 4: Library Management Tools

### 4.1 Resource Tools

**Tool:** `search_library` - Search patterns/templates/snippets
**Tool:** `get_pattern` - Get full pattern definition
**Tool:** `get_snippet` - Get snippet with context adaptation
**Tool:** `get_instructions` - Get step-by-step guide

### 4.2 Library Resource Provider

Expose library as MCP resources:
- `library://patterns` - Pattern index
- `library://pattern/{id}` - Pattern details
- `library://templates` - Template index
- `library://snippets/{category}` - Snippets by category

---

## Phase 5: Code Analysis Engine

### 5.1 Parsers

**Ruby Parser** (tree-sitter-ruby):
- Extract class definitions, methods
- Identify associations, validations, scopes
- Detect concerns and modules

**TypeScript/React Parser** (babel):
- Extract components (functional/class)
- Identify props, state, hooks
- Detect CSS class usage

**CSS Parser** (postcss):
- Extract selectors and properties
- Identify Bootstrap classes
- Detect custom variables

### 5.2 Project Context Detection

**Tool:** `detect_project_context`

Scans project root and returns:
- Rails version, gems installed
- React setup (Vite/Webpack/esbuild)
- Database schema (models, associations)
- Existing components
- CSS framework(s) in use

---

## Phase 6: Learning Engine

### 6.1 Implementation Analysis

**Tool:** `analyze_implementation`

After successful code generation:
- Parse all changed files
- Extract potential patterns/snippets
- Compare against existing library
- Propose contributions

### 6.2 Contribution Workflow

**Tool:** `propose_contribution`
- Validate extracted code
- Generate example usage
- Save to `library/learned/pending_review/`

**Tool:** `review_contributions`
- List pending contributions
- Show diffs and examples

**Tool:** `approve_contribution`
- Move to approved library
- Update indices

**Tool:** `reject_contribution`
- Remove or archive rejected items

---

## Phase 7: Codebase Analyzer (Bootstrap Existing Apps)

### 7.1 Analysis Tools

**Tool:** `analyze_codebase`

Input: path or git URL
Process:
1. Clone if remote, or read local
2. Detect project structure
3. Run all parsers
4. Extract patterns, templates, snippets
5. Generate contribution proposals

**Tool:** `analyze_models`
- Extract all model patterns
- Identify association patterns
- Detect validation patterns
- Generate model templates

**Tool:** `analyze_components`
- Extract React component patterns
- Identify prop patterns
- Detect hook usage patterns
- Generate component templates

**Tool:** `analyze_controllers`
- Extract API endpoint patterns
- Identify authentication patterns
- Detect common action patterns

**Tool:** `analyze_styles`
- Map Bootstrap usage
- Extract color palette
- Identify component styling patterns

### 7.2 Batch Analysis

**Tool:** `batch_analyze`

Input: array of paths/URLs
Process:
1. Analyze each codebase
2. Merge similar patterns
3. Identify common conventions
4. Generate unified library entries

---

## Phase 8: Database Tools

### 8.1 PostgreSQL Tools

**Tool:** `query_database` - Run SELECT queries
**Tool:** `list_tables` - List tables with metadata
**Tool:** `describe_table` - Full table structure
**Tool:** `analyze_query` - EXPLAIN ANALYZE

---

## Phase 9: Starter Library Content

Bootstrap library with essential patterns:

### Patterns (10 initial)
1. `crud-resource` - Basic model + controller + views
2. `nested-resource` - Comments, replies, children
3. `user-authentication` - Login, register, sessions
4. `file-upload` - Active Storage attachments
5. `search-filter` - Search and filter functionality
6. `pagination` - Paginated lists
7. `api-endpoint` - JSON API endpoints
8. `background-job` - Sidekiq/ActiveJob
9. `authorization` - Role-based permissions
10. `bootstrap-to-tailwind` - CSS migration

### Templates (per pattern)
- Model templates
- Migration templates
- Controller templates
- React component templates
- Test templates

### Snippets (30+ initial)
- Authentication helpers
- Form validation
- API response formatters
- React hooks (useAuth, usePagination, etc.)
- Tailwind component classes

---

## Implementation Order

1. **Project setup** - Initialize TS project, install deps
2. **MCP server skeleton** - Basic server with tool registration
3. **Library data structures** - Interfaces, file storage
4. **Template engine** - EJS rendering with helpers
5. **Workflow engine** - Question flow, state management
6. **Basic tools** - identify_intent, start_workflow, execute_workflow
7. **Code parsers** - Ruby, TypeScript, CSS parsers
8. **Analysis tools** - analyze_codebase, extract patterns
9. **Learning engine** - contribution workflow
10. **Starter library** - Initial patterns and templates
11. **Database tools** - PostgreSQL integration
12. **Testing** - Unit tests for engines, integration tests

---

## Files to Create

### Core Server
- `src/index.ts` - Entry point
- `src/server.ts` - Server setup and tool registration

- `src/tools/library.ts` - Library access tools
- `src/tools/analysis.ts` - Codebase analysis tools
- `src/tools/learning.ts` - Contribution tools

- `src/tools/generation.ts` - Code generation tools

### Engines
- `src/engines/WorkflowEngine.ts` - Workflow state machine
- `src/engines/TemplateEngine.ts` - Template rendering
- `src/engines/PatternMatcher.ts` - Intent matching
- `src/engines/CodeAnalyzer.ts` - Multi-language analysis
- `src/engines/ContributionEngine.ts` - Learning logic

### Parsers
- `src/parsers/ruby.ts` - Ruby/Rails parsing
- `src/parsers/typescript.ts` - TS/React parsing
- `src/parsers/css.ts` - CSS/Bootstrap/Tailwind parsing

### Library Structure
- `library/patterns/index.json`
- `library/templates/index.json`
- `library/snippets/index.json`
- `library/patterns/crud-resource/` (example pattern)

### Configuration
- `config/default.yml` - Default configuration
- `package.json` - Dependencies
- `tsconfig.json` - TypeScript config

*/\nexport function calculateSimilarity(str1: string, str2: string): number {\n  const s1 = str1.toLowerCase();\n  const s2 = str2.toLowerCase();\n\n  if (s1 === s2) return 1;\n\n  const words1 = state.currentStepIndex++;\n    state.updatedAt = new Date();\n\n    // Get next step (skipping conditional steps that don't apply)\n    const nextStep = this.getNextStep(state, workflow);\n\n    if step = workflow.steps[state.currentStepIndex];\n\n      // Check condition\n      if (step.condition) {\n        const shouldShow = this.evaluateCondition(step.condition, state);\n        if (!shouldShow) {\n          state.currentStepIndex++;\n          continue;\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Apply context-aware recommendations\n      return this.enhanceStepWithRecommendations(step, state.context);\n    }\n\n    return null;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Enhance a step with context-aware recommendations\n   */\n  private enhanceStepWithRecommendations(\n    step: WorkflowStep,\n    context: ProjectContext\n  ): WorkflowStep {\n    if (!step.options) return step;\n\n    const enhancedOptions = step.options.map((option) => {\n      const enhanced = { ...option };\n\n      // Add recommendations based on context\n      enhanced.recommended = this.shouldRecommend(option, step, context);\n\n      return enhanced;\n    });\n\n    // Sort recommended options first\n    enhancedOptions.sort((a, b) => {\n      if (a.recommended && !b.recommended) return -1;\n      if (!a.recommended && b.recommended) return 1;\n      return 0;\n    });\n\n    return { ...step, options: enhancedOptions };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Determine if an option should be recommended based on context\n   */\n  private shouldRecommend(\n    option: WorkflowOption,\n    step: WorkflowStep,\n    context: ProjectContext\n  ): boolean {\n    // Check for explicit recommendation\n    if (option.recommended) return true;\n\n    // Context-based recommendations\n    const stepId = step.id.toLowerCase();\n    const value = option.value.toLowerCase();\n\n    // Database recommendations\n    if (stepId.includes('database') || stepId.includes('db')) {\n      if (value === 'postgresql' && context.database.adapter === 'postgresql') {\n        return true;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // CSS framework recommendations\n    if (stepId.includes('css') || stepId.includes('style')) {\n      if (value === 'tailwind' && context.cssFramework === 'tailwind') {\n        return true;\n      }\n      if (value === 'bootstrap' && context.cssFramework === 'bootstrap') {\n        return true;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // React hooks recommendations\n    if (stepId.includes('state') || stepId.includes('hook')) {\n      const hasHook = context.hooks.some((h) =>\n        h.name.toLowerCase().includes(value)\n      );\n      if (hasHook) return true;\n    }\n\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Validate an answer against step requirements\n   */\n  private validateAnswer(step: WorkflowStep, answer: unknown): string | null {\n    switch (step.type) {\n      case 'single_select':\n        if (!step.options?.some((o) => o.value === answer)) {\n          return `Invalid option: ${answer}`;\n        }\n        break;\n\n      case 'multi_select':\n        if (!Array.isArray(answer)) {\n          return 'Expected array of selections';\n        }\n        for (const val of answer) {\n          if (!step.options?.some((o) => o.value === val)) {\n            return `Invalid option: ${val}`;\n          }\n        }\n        break;\n\n      case 'text':\n        if (typeof answer !== 'string') {\n          return 'Expected text input';\n        }\n        if (step.validation) {\n          try {\n            const isValid = this.evaluateValidation(step.validation, answer);\n            if (!isValid) {\n              return 'Invalid input format';\n            }\n          } catch {\n            return 'Validation failed';\n          }\n        }\n        break;\n\n      case 'confirm':\n        if (typeof answer !== 'boolean') {\n          return 'Expected boolean confirmation';\n        }\n        break;\n    }\n\n    return null;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Evaluate a condition expression\n   */\n  private evaluateCondition(\n    condition: string,\n    state: WorkflowState\n  ): boolean {\n    try {\n      // Create a safe evaluation context\n      const context = {\n        answers: state.answers,\n        context: state.context,\n        hasModel: (name: string) =>\n          state.context.models.some(\n            (m) => m.name.toLowerCase() === name.toLowerCase()\n          ),\n        hasGem: (name: string) =>\n          state.context.gems.some(\n            (g) => g.name.toLowerCase() === name.toLowerCase()\n          ),\n        hasComponent: (name: string) =>\n          state.context.components.some(\n            (c) => c.name.toLowerCase() === name.toLowerCase()\n          ),\n      };\n\n      // Use Function constructor for sandboxed evaluation\n      const fn = new Function(\n        ...Object.keys(context),\n        `return (${condition})`\n      );\n      return fn(...Object.values(context));\n    } catch {\n      // If evaluation fails, show the step\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Evaluate a validation expression\n   */\n  private evaluateValidation(validation: string, value: string): boolean {\n    try {\n      const fn = new Function('value', `return (${validation})`);\n      return fn(value);\n    } catch {\n      return true;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Generate a summary of the completed workflow\n   */\n  generateSummary(\n    workflowId: string,\n    pattern: Pattern,\n    templates: Template[]\n  ): WorkflowSummary | null {\n    const state = this.activeWorkflows.get(workflowId);\n    if (!state || state.status !== 'ready') {\n      return null;\n    }\n\n    // Determine which templates to use based on answers\n    const selectedTemplates = this.selectTemplates(state, pattern, templates);\n\n    // Get file paths from templates\n    const filesToGenerate = selectedTemplates.map((t) => t.outputPath);\n\n    // Get relevant instructions\n    const instructions = pattern.instructions || [];\n\n    return {\n      patternName: pattern.name,\n      answers: state.answers,\n      filesToGenerate,\n      instructions,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Select templates based on workflow answers\n   */\n  private selectTemplates(\n    state: WorkflowState,\n    pattern: Pattern,\n    allTemplates: Template[]\n  ): Template[] {\n    const selectedIds = new Set<string>(pattern.templates);\n\n    // Add templates from selected options\n    for (const [stepId, answer] of Object.entries(state.answers)) {\n      const step = pattern.workflow.steps.find((s) => s.id === stepId);\n      if (!step?.options) continue;\n\n      const answers = Array.isArray(answer) ? answer : [answer];\n\n      for (const ans of answers) {\n        const option = step.options.find((o) => o.value === ans);\n        if (option?.templates) {\n          option.templates.forEach((t) => selectedIds.add(t));\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    return allTemplates.filter((t) => selectedIds.has(t.id));\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get variables for template rendering from workflow state\n   */\n  getTemplateVariables(workflowId: string): Record<string, unknown> {\n    const state = this.activeWorkflows.get(workflowId);\n    if (!state) return {};\n\n    return {\n      ...state.answers,\n      context: state.context,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Mark workflow as completed\n   */\n  completeWorkflow(workflowId: string): void {\n    const state = this.activeWorkflows.get(workflowId);\n    if (state) {\n      state.status = 'completed';\n      state.updatedAt = new Date();\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Cancel a workflow\n   */\n  cancelWorkflow(workflowId: string): void {\n    const state = this.activeWorkflows.get(workflowId);\n    if (state) {\n      state.status = 'cancelled';\n      state.updatedAt = new Date();\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Clean up old workflows\n   */\n  cleanupOldWorkflows(maxAgeMs: number = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000): void {\n    const now = Date.now();\n\n    for (const [id, state] of this.activeWorkflows.entries()) {\n      if (now - state.updatedAt.getTime() > maxAgeMs) {\n        this.activeWorkflows.delete(id);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Export workflow state for persistence\n   */\n  exportState(workflowId: string): WorkflowState | null {\n    return this.activeWorkflows.get(workflowId) || null;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Import workflow state from persistence\n   */\n  importState(state: WorkflowState): void {\n    this.activeWorkflows.set(state.id, state);\n  }\n}\n"}}]

PatternIndexEntry,\n  IntentMatch,\n} from '../types.js';\nimport { matchTriggers, calculateSimilarity } from '../utils/helpers.js';\n\n/**\n * Pattern Matcher for identifying user intent and matching to patterns\n */\nexport class PatternMatcher {\n  private patterns: Pattern[] = [];\n  private patternIndex: PatternIndexEntry[] = [];\n\n  /**\n   * Load patterns for matching\n   */\n  loadPatterns(patterns: Pattern[]): void {\n    this.patterns = patterns;\n    this.patternIndex = patterns.map((p) => ({\n      id: p.id,\n      name: p.name,\n      category: p.category,\n      triggers: p.triggers,\n      tags: p.tags,\n    }));\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Identify intent from user input\n   */\n  identifyIntent(input: string): IntentMatch | null {\n    const scores: { pattern: Pattern; score: number; matchedTriggers: string[] }[] = [];\n\n    for (const pattern of this.patterns) {\n      const { score, matchedTriggers } = this.scorePattern(input, pattern);\n      if (score > 0.3) {\n        scores.push({ pattern, score, matchedTriggers });\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (scores.length === 0) {\n      return null;\n    }\n\n    // Sort by score descending\n    scores.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);\n\n    const best = scores[0];\n\n    // Get alternative patterns (score > 0.5 and within 0.2 of best)\n    const alternativePatterns = scores\n      .slice(1)\n      .filter((s) => s.score > 0.5 && best.score - s.score < 0.2)\n      .map((s) => ({\n        patternId: s.pattern.id,\n        confidence: s.score,\n      }));\n\n    return {\n      patternId: best.pattern.id,\n      confidence: best.score,\n      matchedTriggers: best.matchedTriggers,\n      alternativePatterns:\n        alternativePatterns.length > 0 ? alternativePatterns : undefined,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Score a pattern against user input\n   */\n  private scorePattern(\n    input: string,\n    pattern: Pattern\n  ): { score: number; matchedTriggers: string[] } {\n    const inputLower = input.toLowerCase();\n    const matchedTriggers: string[] = [];\n    let maxScore = 0;\n\n    // Check triggers\n    for (const trigger of pattern.triggers) {\n      const triggerLower = trigger.toLowerCase();\n\n      // Exact phrase match\n      if (inputLower.includes(triggerLower)) {\n        matchedTriggers.push(trigger);\n        maxScore = Math.max(maxScore, 1.0);\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      // Word overlap scoring\n      const triggerScore = matchTriggers(input, [trigger]);\n      if (triggerScore > 0.5) {\n        matchedTriggers.push(trigger);\n        maxScore = Math.max(maxScore, triggerScore);\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Check pattern name\n    const nameScore = calculateSimilarity(input, pattern.name);\n    if (nameScore > 0.5) {\n      maxScore = Math.max(maxScore, nameScore * 0.8);\n    }\n\n    // Check tags\n    for (const tag of pattern.tags) {\n      if (inputLower.includes(tag.toLowerCase())) {\n        maxScore = Math.max(maxScore, 0.6);\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Check category keywords\n    const categoryKeywords = this.getCategoryKeywords(pattern.category);\n    for (const keyword of categoryKeywords) {\n      if (inputLower.includes(keyword)) {\n        maxScore = Math.max(maxScore, 0.5);\n      }\n    }\n\n    return { score: maxScore, matchedTriggers };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get keywords associated with a category\n   */\n  private getCategoryKeywords(category: string): string[] {\n    const keywords: Record<string, string[]> = {\n      model: ['model', 'table', 'database', 'schema', 'activerecord'],\n      controller: ['controller', 'action', 'endpoint', 'route'],\n      view: ['view', 'page', 'template', 'erb'],\n      component: ['component', 'react', 'ui', 'widget'],\n      authentication: score };\n    });\n\n    return scored\n      .filter((s) => s.score > 0.2)\n      .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)\n      .slice(0, limit)\n      .map((s) => s.entry);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get a suggestRelated(patternId: string, limit: number = 5): Pattern[] {\n    const pattern = this.getPattern(patternId);\n    if (!pattern) return [];\n\n    const scored = this.patterns\n      .filter((p) (c) => c.name === controllerName\n      );\n\n      if (!controller) continue;\n\n      // Check for standard CRUD actions\n      const crudActions = ['index', 'show', 'new', 'create', 'edit',   sourceFile: model.filePath,\n      generatedTemplate: template,\n      variables: [\n        { name: 'modelName', type: 'string', required: true },\n        { name: 'associations', type: 'object', required: false },\n        { name: 'validations', type: 'object', required: false },\n      ],\n      confidence: 0.7,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Generalize Ruby code into template\n   */\n  private generalizeRubyCode(code: string, className: string): string {\n    let template = code;\n\n    // Replace class name\n    template = template.replace(\n      new RegExp(`class\\\\s+${className}`, component: ComponentInfo\n  ): Promise<ExtractedTemplate> {\n    const content = await readFile(component.filePath);\n\n    const template = this.generalizeTypeScriptCode(content, component.name);\n\n    return {\n      suggestedId: `component-${underscore(component.name)}`,\n      name: `${component.name} Component`,\n      category: 'component',\n      sourceFile: component.filePath,\n      generatedTemplate: template,\n      variables: [\n        { name: 'componentName', type: 'string', required: true },\n        { name: 'props', type: 'array', required: false },\n      ],\n      confidence: 0.7,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Generalize TypeScript code into template\n   */\n  private generalizeTypeScriptCode(code: string, componentName: string): string {\n    let template = code;\n\n    // Replace component name\n    template = template.replace(\n      new RegExp(`\\\\b${componentName}\\\\b`, 'g'),\n      '<%= componentName %>'\n    );\n\n    return template;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Extract snippets from codebase\n   */\n  private async extractSnippets(\n    projectPath: string,\n    context: ProjectContext\n  ): Promise<ExtractedSnippet[]> {\n    const snippets: ExtractedSnippet[] = [];\n\n    // Extract validation snippets\n    const validationSnippets = this.extractValidationSnippets(context.models);\n    snippets.push(...validationSnippets);\n\n    // Extract association snippets\n    const associationSnippets = this.extractAssociationSnippets(context.models);\n    snippets.push(...associationSnippets);\n\n    // Extract hook snippets\n    const hookSnippets = this.extractHookSnippets(context.hooks);\n    snippets.push(...hookSnippets);\n\n    return snippets;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Extract validation snippets from models\n   */\n  private extractValidationSnippets(models: ModelInfo[]): ExtractedSnippet[] {\n    const snippets: ExtractedSnippet[] = [];\n    const validationCounts = new Map<string, number>();\n\n    for (const model of models) {\n      for (const validation of model.validations) {\n        const key = validation.type;\n        validationCounts.set(key, (validationCounts.get(key) || 0) + 1);\n      }\n    }\n\n    for (const [type, count] of validationCounts) {\n      if (count >= 2) {\n        snippets.push({\n          suggestedId: `validation-${type}`,\n          name: `${camelize(type)} Validation`,\n          category: 'validation',\n          sourceFile: 'multiple',\n          code: `validates :{{field}}, ${type}: true`,\n          usageCount: count,\n          confidence: Math.min(count / 5, 1),\n        });\n      }\n    }\n\n    return snippets;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Extract association snippets from models\n   */\n  private extractAssociationSnippets(models: ModelInfo[]): ExtractedSnippet[] {\n    const snippets: ExtractedSnippet[] = [];\n    const associationPatterns = new Map<string, { count: number; example: string }>();\n\n    for (const model of models) {\n      for (const assoc of model.associations) {\n        const key = assoc.type;\n        const example = `${assoc.type} :${assoc.name}`;\n\n        const existing = associationPatterns.get(key);\n        if (existing) {\n          existing.count++;\n        } else {\n          associationPatterns.set(key, { count: 1, example });\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    for (const [type, data] of associationPatterns) {\n      snippets.push({\n        suggestedId: `association-${type.replace(/_/g, '-')}`,\n        name: `${camelize(type)} Association`,\n        category: 'association',\n        sourceFile: 'multiple',\n        code: `${type} :{{name}}`,\n        usageCount: data.count,\n        confidence: Math.min(data.count / 5, 1),\n      });\n    }\n\n    return snippets;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Extract hook snippets\n   */\n  private extractHookSnippets(hooks: HookInfo[]): ExtractedSnippet[] {\n    return hooks.map((hook) => ({\n      suggestedId: `hook-${underscore(hook.name)}`,\n      name: hook.name,\n      category: 'hook',\n      sourceFile: hook.filePath,\n      code: `import { ${hook.name} } from './hooks/${hook.name}'`,\n      usageCount: 1,\n      confidence: 0.5,\n    }));\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * findFiles('**/*.rb', projectPath),\n      findFiles('**/*.{ts,tsx}', projectPath),\n      findFiles('**/*.{css,scss}', projectPath),\n    ]);\n\n    const models = await this.rubyParser.parseAllModels(projectPath);\n    const controllers = await this.rubyParser.parseAllControllers(projectPath);\n    const components = await this.tsParser.parseAllComponents(projectPath);\n    const hooks = await this.tsParser.parseAllHooks(projectPath);\n\n    return {\n      totalFiles: rubyFiles.length + tsFiles.length + cssFiles.length,\n      rubyFiles: rubyFiles.length,\n      typeScriptFiles: tsFiles.length,\n      cssFiles: cssFiles.length,\n      modelsFound: models.length,\n      controllersFound: controllers.length,\n      componentsFound: components.length,\n      hooksFound: hooks.length,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Analyze models specifically\n   */\n  async analyzeModels(projectPath: string): Promise<ModelInfo[]> {\n    return this.rubyParser.parseAllModels(projectPath);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Analyze components specifically\n   */\n  async analyzeComponents(projectPath: string): Promise<ComponentInfo[]> {\n    return this.tsParser.parseAllComponents(projectPath);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Analyze controllers specifically\n   */\n  async analyzeControllers(projectPath: string): Promise<ControllerInfo[]> {\n    return this.rubyParser.parseAllControllers(projectPath);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Analyze styles specifically\n   */\n  async analyzeStyles(projectPath: string): Promise<{\n    framework: string;\n    classes: string[];\n    variables: Record<string, string>;\n  }> {\n    const framework = await this.cssParser.detectFramework(projectPath);\n    const classes = await this.cssParser.getAllCustomStyles(projectPath);\n    const colorPalette = await this.cssParser.extractColorPalette(projectPath);\n\n    return {\n      framework,\n      classes,\n      variables: colorPalette,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Batch analyze multiple codebases\n   */\n  async batchAnalyze(pathsOrUrls: string[]): Promise<AnalysisResult[]> {\n    const results: AnalysisResult[] = [];\n\n    for (const pathOrUrl of pathsOrUrls) {\n      try {\n        const result = await this.analyzeCodebase(pathOrUrl);\n        results.push(result);\n      } catch (error) {\n        console.error(`Failed to analyze ${pathOrUrl}:`, error);\n      }\n    }\n\n    return results;\n  }\n}\n"}}]

   .map((p) => p.name);\n\n      return {\n        matched: false,\n        suggestions: suggestions.length > 0 ? suggestions : undefined,\n      };\n    }\n\n    const pattern = const candidates = [\n        { patternId: match.patternId, confidence: match.confidence },\n        ...match.alternativePatterns,\n      ];\n\n      const clarifying = this.patternMatcher.generateClarifyingQuestions(\n        input.prompt,\n        candidates\n      );\n\n      return {\n        matched: true,\n        patternId: match.patternId,\n        patternName: pattern?.name,\n        confidence: match.confidence,\n        clarifyingQuestion: clarifying,\n      };\n    }\n\n    const alternatives = match.alternativePatterns?.map((alt) => {\n      const p = this.patternMatcher.getPattern(alt.patternId);\n      return {\n        patternId: alt.patternId,\n        name: p?.name || alt.patternId,\n        confidence: alt.confidence,\n      };\n modelCount: context.models.length,\n        componentCount: context.components.length,\n      },\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Answer a workflow step\n   */\n  async answerStep(input: );\n\n    if (result.validationError) {\n      return {\n        success: false,\n        completed: false,\n        validationError: result.validationError,\n      };\n    }\n\n    if (result.completed) {\n      // Generate summary\n      const templates = await this.getPatternTemplates(pattern);\n      const summary = this.workflowEngine.generateSummary(\n        input.workflowId,\n        pattern,\n        templates\n      );\n\n      return {\n        success: true,\n        completed: true,\n        summary: summary || undefined,\n      };\n    }\n\n Pattern): Promise<any[]> {\n    // This would load templates from the library\n    // For now, return empty array\n    return [];\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Execute a completed workflow\n   */\n  async this.patternMatcher.getPattern(state.patternId);\n\n    if (!pattern) {\n      return {\n        success: false,\n        error: 'Pattern not found',\n      };\n    }\n\n    const variables = this.workflowEngine.getTemplateVariables(input.workflowId);\n    const generatedFiles: Array<{ path: string; content: string }> = [];\n\n    // Get templates and render them\n    const templates = (!input.dryRun) {\n          // In production, we'd write files here\n          // For now, just collect them\n        }\n\n        generatedFiles.push({\n          path: rendered.path,\n          content: rendered.content,\n        });\n      } catch (error) {\n        const err = error as Error;\n        return {\n          success: false,\n          error: `Failed to render template ${template.id}: ${err.message}`,\n        };\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Mark workflow as completed\n    if (!input.dryRun) {\n      this.workflowEngine.completeWorkflow(input.workflowId);\n    }\n\n    return {\n      success: true,\n      generatedFiles,\n      instructions: pattern.instructions,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Cancel an active workflow\n   */\n  cancelWorkflow(input: CancelWorkflowInput): { success: boolean; error?: string } {\n    const state = this.workflowEngine.getWorkflowState(input.workflowId);\n\n    if (!state) {\n      return { success: false, error: 'Workflow not found' };\n    }\n\n    this.workflowEngine.cancelWorkflow(input.workflowId);\n\n    return { success: true };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get current workflow state\n   */\n templateResult.template;\n\n      try {\n        const rendered = await this.templateEngine.renderTemplate(\n          template,\n          input.variables\n        );\n\n        const outputPath = path.join(input.basePath, rendered.path);\n\n        let written = false;\n        if (!input.dryRun) {\n          await ensureDirectory(path.dirname(outputPath));\n          await writeFile(outputPath, rendered.content);\n          written = true;\n        }\n\n        results.push({\n          templateId,\n          path: outputPath,\n          content: rendered.content,\n          written,\n        });\n      } catch (error) {\n        const err = error as Error;\n        errors.push({\n          templateId,\n          error: err.message,\n        });\n      }\n    }\n\n    return {\n      success: errors.length === 0,\n      results,\n      errors: errors.length > 0 ? errors : undefined,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Generate all files for a pattern\n   */\n  async generateFromPattern(input: GenerateFromPatternInput): Promise<{\n    success: boolean;\n    results?: Array<{\n      templateId: string;\n      path: string;\n      content: string;\n      written: boolean;\n    }>;\n    instructions?: string[];\n    errors?: Array<{\n      templateId: string;\n      error: string;\n    }>;\n  }> {\n    // Get pattern from library\n    const patternResult = await this.libraryTools.getPattern({\n      patternId: input.patternId,\n    });\n\n    if (!patternResult.found || !patternResult.pattern) {\n      return {\n        success: false,\n        errors: [{ templateId: input.patternId, error: 'Pattern not found' }],\n      };\n    }\n\n    const pattern = patternResult.pattern;\n\n    // Generate all templates for the pattern\n    const multipleResult = await this.generateMultiple({\n      templateIds: pattern.templates,\n      variables: input.variables,\n      basePath: input.projectPath,\n      dryRun: input.dryRun,\n    });\n\n    return {\n      success: multipleResult.success,\n      results: multipleResult.results,\n      instructions: pattern.instructions,\n      errors: multipleResult.errors,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Render a snippet with variables\n   */\n  async renderSnippet(input: RenderSnippetInput): Promise<{\n    success: boolean;\n    result?: {\n      originalCode: string;\n      renderedCode: string;\n    };\n    error?: string;\n  }> {\n    const snippetResult = await this.libraryTools.getSnippet({\n      snippetId: input.snippetId,\n      variables: input.variables,\n    });\n\n    if (!snippetResult.found || !snippetResult.snippet) {\n      return {\n        success: false,\n        error: `Snippet not found: ${input.snippetId}`,\n      };\n    }\n\n    return {\n      success: true,\n      result: {\n        originalCode: snippetResult.snippet.code,\n        renderedCode: snippetResult.renderedCode || snippetResult.snippet.code,\n      },\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Validate variables for a template\n   */\n  async validateTemplateVariables(input: ValidateTemplateVariablesInput): Promise<{\n    valid: boolean;\n    errors?: string[];\n    missingRequired?: string[];\n    typeErrors?: Array<{\n      variable: string;\n      expected: string;\n      got: string;\n    }>;\n  }> {\n    const templateResult = await this.libraryTools.getTemplate({\n      templateId: input.templateId,\n    });\n\n    if (!templateResult.found || !templateResult.template) {\n      return {\n        valid: false,\n        errors: [`Template not found: ${input.templateId}`],\n      };\n    }\n\n    const template = templateResult.template;\n    const errors: string[] = [];\n    const missingRequired: string[] = [];\n    const typeErrors: Array<{ variable: string; expected: string; got: string }> = [];\n\n    for (const varDef of template.variables) {\n      const value = input.variables[varDef.name];\n\n      // Check required\n      if (varDef.required && (value === undefined || value === null)) {\n        missingRequired.push(varDef.name);\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      // Check type\n      if (value !== undefined && value !== null) {\n        const actualType = Array.isArray(value) ? 'array' : typeof value;\n        if (actualType !== varDef.type && varDef.type !== 'object') {\n          typeErrors.push({\n            variable: varDef.name,\n            expected: varDef.type,\n            got: actualType,\n          });\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    const valid = missingRequired.length === 0 && typeErrors.length === 0;\n\n    return {\n      valid,\n      errors: errors.length > 0 ? errors : undefined,\n      missingRequired: missingRequired.length > 0 ? missingRequired : undefined,\n      typeErrors: typeErrors.length > 0 ? typeErrors : undefined,\n    };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Check if a file would be overwritten\n   */\n  async checkConflicts(paths: string[]): Promise<{\n    conflicts: string[];\n    safe: string[];\n  }> {\n    const conflicts: string[] = [];\n    const safe: string[] = [];\n\n    for (const filePath of paths) {\n      if (await fileExists(filePath)) {\n        conflicts.push(filePath);\n      } else {\n        safe.push(filePath);\n      }\n    }\n\n    return { conflicts, safe };\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Get tool definitions for MCP registration\n   */\n  static getToolDefinitions() {\n    return [\n      {\n        name: (!templateResult.found || !templateResult.template) {\n        errors.push({\n          templateId,\n          error: `Template not found: ${templateId}`,\n        });\n        continue;\n      }\n\n writeFile(outputPath, rendered.content);\n          written = true;\n        }\n\n        results.push({\n          templateId,\n          path: outputPath,\n          content: rendered.content,\n This server provides guided workflows, code generation from templates, and learns from successful implementations to improve its library over time.\n\n## Features\n\n- **Workflow Engine**: Guides users through code generation with questions and options\n- **Pattern Library**: Pre-built patterns for common Rails/React development tasks\n- **Template Engine**: EJS-based templates with Rails/React convention helpers\n- **Code Analysis**: Parse and analyze existing codebases to extract patterns\n- **Learning Engine**: Learn from successful implementations to improve the library\n- **PostgreSQL Integration**: Query and analyze your database directly\n\n## Installation\n\n```bash\nnpm install\nnpm run build\n```\n\n## Usage\n\n### As an MCP Server\n\nAdd to your Claude Code MCP settings:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"mcpServers\": {\n    \"rails-dev\": {\n      \"command\": \"node\",\n      \"args\": [\"/path/to/rails-dev-mcp/dist/index.js\"],\n      \"env\": {\n        \"RAILS_MCP_LIBRARY\": \"/path/to/rails-dev-mcp/library\"\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Command Line Options\n\n```bash\nnode dist/index.js --help\n\nOptions:\n  --library <path>  Path to the library directory (default: ./library)\n  --config <path>   Path to configuration file (default: ./config/default.yml)\n  --help            Show help\n```\n\n### Environment Variables\n\n- `RAILS_MCP_LIBRARY` - PostgreSQL password\n- `RAILS_MCP_DB_NAME` - PostgreSQL database\n\n## Available Tools\n\n### Workflow Tools\n- `identify_intent` - Match user intent to patterns\n- `start_workflow` - Begin a guided workflow\n- `answer_workflow_step` - Answer workflow questions\n- `execute_workflow` - Generate code from completed workflow\n- `cancel_workflow` - Cancel active workflow\n\n### Library Tools\n- `search_library` - Search patterns, templates, snippets\n- `get_pattern` - Get pattern definition\n- `get_template` - Get template with content\n- `get_snippet` - Get snippet with variable substitution\n- `list_patterns` - List all patterns\n- `list_templates` - List all templates\n- `list_snippets` - List all snippets\n\n### Analysis Tools\n- `detect_project_context` - Analyze project structure\n- `analyze_codebase` - Full codebase analysis\n- `analyze_models` - Analyze Rails models\n- `analyze_components` - Analyze React components\n- `analyze_controllers` - Analyze Rails controllers\n- `analyze_styles` - Analyze CSS/styling\n- `batch_analyze` - Analyze multiple projects\n\n### Learning Tools\n- `analyze_implementation` - Propose new patterns from code\n- `propose_contribution` - Submit new pattern/template/snippet\n- `review_contributions` - List pending contributions\n- `approve_contribution` - Approve and add to library\n- `reject_contribution` - Reject contribution\n\n### Database Tools\n- `query_database` - Run SELECT queries\n- `list_tables` - List database tables\n- `describe_table` - Get table structure\n- `analyze_query` - EXPLAIN ANALYZE\n- `table_stats` - Get table statistics\n\n### Generation Tools\n- `generate_from_template` - Generate single file\n- `generate_multiple` - Generate multiple files\n- `generate_from_pattern` - Generate all pattern files\n- `render_snippet` - Render snippet with variables\n\n## Included Patterns\n\n1. **crud-resource** - Full CRUD with model, controller, React components\n2. **nested-resource** - Comments, replies, child resources\n3. **user-authentication** - Login, signup, sessions\n4. **file-upload** - Active Storage attachments\n5. **search-filter** - Search and filtering\n6. **pagination** - Paginated lists\n7. **api-endpoint** - JSON API endpoints\n8. **background-job** - Sidekiq/ActiveJob\n9. **authorization** - Role-based permissions\n10. **bootstrap-to-tailwind** - CSS migration\n\n## Library Structure\n\n```\nlibrary/\n├── patterns/\n│   ├── index.json\n│   └── {pattern-id}/\n│       └── manifest.json\n├── templates/\n│   ├── index.json\n│   ├── {template-id}.json\n│   └── {template-id}.ejs\n├── snippets/\n│   ├── index.json\n│   └── {snippet-id}.json\n└── learned/\n    ├── pending_review/\n    ├── approved/\n    └── rejected/\n```\n\n## Extending the Library\n\n### Adding a Pattern\n\nCreate a new directory under `library/patterns/` with a `manifest.json`:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"id\": \"my-pattern\",\n  \"name\": \"My Pattern\",\n  \"description\": \"Description of the pattern\",\n  \"category\": \"full-stack\",\n  \"triggers\": [\"keywords\", \"to match\"],\n  \"workflow\": {\n    \"id\": \"wf-my-pattern\",\n    \"steps\": [...]\n  },\n  \"templates\": [\"template-ids\"],\n  \"snippets\": [\"snippet-ids\"],\n  \"instructions\": [\"Post-generation steps\"],\n  \"version\": \"1.0.0\",\n  \"tags\": [\"tags\"]\n}\n```\n\n### Adding a Template\n\nCreate JSON metadata and EJS template files:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"id\": \"my-template\",\n  \"name\": \"My Template\",\n  \"category\": \"model\",\n  \"language\": \"ruby\",\n  \"filePath\": \"templates/my-template.ejs\",\n  \"outputPath\": \"app/models/<%= underscore(name) %>.rb\",\n  \"variables\": [\n    {\"name\": \"name\", \"type\": \"string\", \"required\": true}\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Adding a Snippet\n\n```json\n{\n  \"id\": \"my-snippet\",\n  \"name\": \"My Snippet\",\n  \"category\": \"validation\",\n  \"language\": \"ruby\",\n  \"code\": \"validates {{field}}, presence: true\",\n  \"variables\": [\n    {\"name\": \"field\", \"description\": \"Field name\"}\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n## Development\n\n```bash\n# Build\nnpm run build\n\n# Watch mode\nnpm run dev\n\n# Run tests\nnpm test\n```\n\n## License\n\nMIT\n"}}]

## assistant

[{"type":"text","text":"The `claude export` command has different syntax. Try checking the help:\n\n```bash\nclaude export --help\n```\n\nBut the simplest workaround is to just convert the JSONL file directly:\n\n```bash\ncat 3fbf8670-5e46-4dfd-938f-58e583da3273.jsonl | jq -r '\n  select(.type == \"user\" or .type == \"assistant\") | \n  \"## \\(.type | ascii_upcase)\\n\\n\\(.message.content // .content // \"\")\\n\\n---\\n\"\n' > ~/mcp-servers/rails-dev-mcp/feb2-1.md\n```\n\nOr if the JSON structure is different:\n\n```bash\njq -r 'to_entries | .[] | \"\\(.key): \\(.value)\"' 3fbf8670-5e46-4dfd-938f-58e583da3273.jsonl > ~/mcp-servers/rails-dev-mcp/feb2-1.txt\n```\n\nIf those don't work well, you can just copy the raw file and read it later:\n\n```bash\ncp 3fbf8670-5e46-4dfd-938f-58e583da3273.jsonl ~/mcp-servers/rails-dev-mcp/feb2-1.jsonl\n```"}]
